影响战斗能力。	Affects combat prowess.
对灵气的感知能力，影响灵气护盾穿透率，法宝镇压几率。	The ability to perceive Qi. Affects Qi Barrier Penetration Chance and Artifact Suppression Chance.
影响角色之间互动事件发生的概率，招募角色的概率等。	Affects the chance of events triggering during interactions between characters and the chance of recruiting new characters.
对自身身体了解掌控的能力，影响淬体效率，淬体时出现有效进化的概率。在凡人阶段的岐黄技能会一定程度上影响该值。	The ability to comprehend and command one's own body. Affects Remold efficiency, as well as chance of an effective evolution to occur when Remolding. One's Healing skill as a mortal will affect this value to some extent.
影响烹饪速度，烹饪成功率等。	Affects speed and success rate when cooking.
影响建筑速度，建筑受伤时的概率等。	Affects speed and chances of being injured during construction work.
影响种植作物速度，收获作物产量等。	Affects the growth rate of crops and their harvest yield.
影响采掘速度，采掘产量等。	Affects speed and output of mining.
对灵感的把握能力，影响淬体时高级进化方向的出现概率。	The ability to handle inspirations. Affects the chance of advanced Evolution Directions to occur in Remolding.
对世界万物规律的理解能力，影响吐纳和吞噬获得精华的效率。在凡人阶段的巧匠技能会一定程度上影响该值。	The ability to comprehend the laws of everything in nature. Affects the efficiency of gaining essence by Breathing and Devouring. One's Crafting skill as a mortal will affect this value to a certain extent.
影响进入内门时，御物，术法，护体的初始等级。	Affects the initial level of Artifact Mastery, Spell and Protection when a character becomes an inner disciple.
影响岐黄，巧匠技巧，在进入内门时转化为炼丹，炼器的比例。	Affects healing and crafting skill. These will be converted into Alchemy and Artifact Crafting when a character becomes an inner disciple.

角色对外界的探查与反馈的能力，影响角色的视野，以及需要精细工作的效率等属性。	Perception (PER): A character's ability to explore and gather intelligence from the outside world. Affects a character's field of vision and their efficiency of fine work.
角色身体的强度，影响角色的寿命，抗寒抗热，以及与体力相关的效率等属性。	Constitution (CON): The strength of a character's body. Affects a character's lifespan, cold and heat resistance and efficiency when it comes to physical labor.
角色获取他人好感的能力，包括外在容貌与内在气质，影响角色的社交能力。	Charisma (CHA): A character's ability to gain favor from others, including their appearance and disposition. Affects a character's social ability.
角色思考的能力，影响角色的学习速度等属性。	Intelligence (INT): A character's ability to think. Affects the speed of learning.
角色受上天眷顾的程度，影响角色概率相关的属性。	Luck (LUK): The extent to which a character is favored by the Heaven. Affects stats related to chance.
角色在修炼上的潜在能力。潜力与角色的年龄与个人经历有关，一旦进入内门就会锁定，无法被改变。	Potential (POT): A character's training potential. Potential is related to the age and background of a character. Once a character becomes an inner disciple, this will be locked and cannot be changed further.

你的情感依然很丰富，依然会被喜怒哀乐所动。这些凡人的情感让你对神力的掌握倍加艰难，但也正因如此，就算是很平凡很微小的信仰你都能感受并收取。	You still have many human emotions such as joy, anger and sorrow. These human emotions have made it difficult for you to master divine powers, but at the same time, you can feel and absorb even the slightest mortal belief.
你对凡人的情感逐渐收敛，已经很少会有极端的狂喜或悲恸。得益于此，你对神力的掌握渐渐加深，但来自众生的那些平凡微小的信仰你已无法尽数感知。	You have less human emotions and can hardly feel extreme joy or sorrow. You have become more attuned to divine powers, but can no longer perceive all the mortal and small beliefs.
凡人的喜怒哀乐对你的影响越来越少，而你对神力的运用也渐入佳境。但逐渐失去凡人心态的你也越发难以吸收那些平凡而普通的信仰。	Human emotions affect you less and less, and you begin to master divine powers. But your loss of humanity has rendered you less perceptive to human beliefs.
你的情感已经十分淡漠，很少有什么事可以让你动容。你对神力的运用越发自如，但来自诸多平凡信众的信仰对你而言已近乎尘砾。	You have become very indifferent toward people and worldly affairs. You are more in tune with divine powers, but ordinary people's beliefs are almost nothing to you.

在游戏中，玩家不能直接控制角色，大部分交互指令都是通过命令指定的方式下达。\n点击对应功能按钮后选择交互对象，即可完成交互指令的下达。	Characters cannot be controlled directly, instead, most interactions are done by giving them orders.\nClick a function and select the target character(s) to complete the order.

游戏中的资源采集，也通过命令下达的方式来完成。\n游戏中针对不同的资源拥有不同的命令。\n例如[开采]对应[矿石]，[砍伐]对应[树木]。	Collecting resources is also done by issuing orders.\nDifferent resources have different orders.\nFor example, [Mine] is for [Ores], and [Chop] is for [Trees].

建筑是发展门派的核心内容。使用主材料的不同，建筑也会拥有不同的属性，并以此来影响周围的环境。\n例如：寒晶锭建造的建筑，会使周围的水属性增多。	Structures are the core of developing a sect. A building's attribute depends on the main material used in the construction, and its attribute also affects the surrounding environment.\nFor example, a structure made from Ice Crystal Bars will increase the surrounding Water attribute.
五行是游戏世界的重要元素，五行生克影响游戏的方方面面。如[color=#ff0000]境界突破[/color]，[color=#ff0000]建筑风水[/color]，[color=#ff0000]法宝炼制[/color]等等。	The Five Elements are an important part of this world. The interactions between the elements affect the entire world: [color=#ff0000]Breakthrough[/color], [color=#ff0000]Feng Shui[/color], [color=#ff0000]Artifact Crafting[/color], etc.
以建筑风水为例：\n[color=#ff0000]火属性[/color]的建筑在[color=#ff0000]水属性[/color]的环境中，就会因[color=#ff0000]水克火[/color]的原因而风水不好。\n[color=#ff0000]火属性[/color]的建筑在[color=#ff0000]木属性[/color]的环境中，因[color=#ff0000]木生火[/color]之故，风水就会很棒。	Take structure Feng Shui as an example: \n[color=#ff0000]Fire[/color]-element buildings in a [color=#ff0000]Water[/color]-element environment will have bad Feng Shui as [color=#ff0000]Water extinguishes Fire[/color].\n[color=#ff0000]Fire[/color]-element buildings in a [color=#ff0000]Wood[/color]-element environment will have great Feng Shui as [color=#ff0000]Wood fuels Fire[/color].
再以境界突破为例：\n[color=#ff0000]木属性[/color]的功法在[color=#ff0000]金属性[/color]的环境中突破时，因[color=#ff0000]金克木[/color]的原因而倍加艰难。\n如果在[color=#ff0000]水属性[/color]的环境中突破，则会因[color=#ff0000]水生木[/color]之故，而提高突破成功率。	And when performing Breakthrough for a State:\nPracticing a Law of [color=#ff0000]Wood[/color] in an environment of [color=#ff0000]Metal[/color] will be difficult because [color=#ff0000]Metal cuts Wood[/color].\nIf one instead does it an environment of [color=#ff0000]Water[/color], the success rate of a Breakthrough will increase because [color=#ff0000]Water nourishes Wood[/color].
在掌门附近，发布一个寒晶鼎的建造命令。	Order the construction of an Ice Crystal Cauldron next to the sect leader.

工作计划是外门的核心策略模块，规定了外门弟子的工作优先级和重心。\n工作优先级越往右越低，可以进行高优先级工作时不会进行低优先级工作。\n[color=#9e6404][特别优先]可以将一个工作优先级提高到所有工作之上[/color]。	Work schedule is a core strategic function in which you can establish a set of priorities for outer disciples.\nThe priorities are listed from left to right. A task with a lower priority will only be done if there are no other performable tasks of higher priority.\n[color=#9e6404][Top Priority] allows a task to take precedence over all other tasks[/color].
在工作计划面板中，为角色勾选[筑工]。	Head to Schedule and Select [Builder] for the character.

吐纳	Breathing
前往目标地点吐纳天地之间的元气，以获得淬体所需的淬炼精华。吐纳时的季节、时间、天气、环境等均会影响吐纳获得精华的种类和效率。	Go to the target location and breath the primordial Qi between heaven and earth in order to obtain the Essence needed for Remolding. 炼制圣物	Craft Sacred Relic

Metal and Water count as Yin and have a bonus effect at night. Earth requires a balanced Yin and Yang.

所谓风水，指的是目标建筑五行属性，与所在位置五行分布的融洽关系。\n例如：[color=#ff0000]火属性[/color]的建筑在[color=#ff0000]水属性[/color]的环境中，就会因[color=#ff0000]水克火[/color]的原因而风水不好。\n[color=#ff0000]火属性[/color]的建筑在[color=#ff0000]木属性[/color]的环境中，因[color=#ff0000]木生火[/color]之故，风水就会很棒。\n在屏幕左上角可以随时查看五行生克关系。	Feng Shui refers to a building's element and the harmonic balance of the location's five elements.\nExample: [color=#ff0000]Fire[/color]-element buildings in a [color=#ff0000]Water[/color]-element environment will have bad Feng Shui as [color=#ff0000]Water extinguishes Fire[/color].\n[color=#ff0000]Fire[/color]-element buildings in a [color=#ff0000]Wood[/color]-element environment will have great Feng Shui as [color=#ff0000]Wood fuels Fire[/color].\nYou can view how the five elements interact with each other at any time in the top-left corner.
你可以通过屏幕左上角的太极图来进入风水视图，在风水试图下，屏幕中央的五边形即为鼠标所在位置的五行分布。	You can enter Feng Shui View via the Taiji icon in the top-left corner. When using Feng Shui View, pointing your cursor at anything will display a five elements layout of the area.
[color=#ff0000]装饰性建筑[/color]/[color=#ff0000]地板[/color]/[color=#ff0000]墙壁[/color]根据其主材料不同可以改变附近的五行分布，请尝试使用合适的材料去改换床铺附近的建筑，使之风水化凶为吉。	Depending on the material used for [color=#ff0000]Decorations[/color]/[color=#ff0000]Floor[/color]/[color=#ff0000]Walls[/color], you can change the vicinity's five element flow.
